 jammu-kashmir hoicourt ne khuli adaalat main ek teacher se gaay par niabandh likhane or chauthi class ke ganit ke sawaal hal karne ko kaha or jab vah in donon kaamon ko karne main vifal rahe to jaj ne 'nirdayee' prashasan se shiksha kii 'dukaanon' ko band karne ko kaha
 Justice Muzaffar Hussain Atar was hearing a petition challenging the appointment of Mohammad Imran Khan as rahbar-e-talim (education Guide) at a school in southern Kashmir on Friday
 yachikakarta ne aarope lagaaya tha ki ucchtar madhyamik shiksha board dilli or global open uniwarsity, nagaland dwaara jari khan ke praaanpatr manyata praapt nahin hai
 The marksheet released by the Delhi Board shows that Mohammad scored 74 per cent, 73 per cent and 66 per cent in Urdu, English and Mathematics respectively
 adaalat ne ek varisht vakil se kaha ki vah mohammad ko ek saadhaaran pankti kaa angreji se urdu or urdu se angreji main anuwaad karne ko den, lekin vah aisa karne main vifal rahe
 After this, the teacher was given to write an essay on cow in Urdu, but he could not write it either
 mohammad ne adaalat kaksh se baahar jaakar niabandh likhane kii anumati maangi, lekin manjuuri milane ke baad bhi vah niabandh nahin likh paae
 Mohammed, who claimed to have a good grasp of mathematics, was given a fourth grade mathematics question to solve
 uske phir se fail hone par vyathit najar aa rahe nyaayadhish atar ne kaha, 'aisi surat main, rajya kaa bhavishya kya hoga iskaa andaja lagaaya ja saktaa he
 School going children
 
 
 paas hokar bhi murkh hi bane rahenge
 ' adaalat ne apni tippanee main kaha, 'jammu-kashmir rajya main prashasan par yah sunishchit karne kii jimmedaari he ki shiksha or shikshavidon kaa kshetra pradooshit nahin ho, lekin is maamle main saamne aae tathyon ko dekhte hue pataa chalata he ki prashasan ne vivekahin nikaay or aankh moond kar kaam kiya he, kyonki unhone academik digriyon ko hasil karne main hui bhayanak galatiyon ko nazarandaaj kar aapraadhik bhul kii he
 'judge Atar called the study centers providing certificates to ineligible candidates a' sweet shop '
 unhone kaha, 'maujuuda rit yachika academik digriyon kii kharid farokht kaa chaukaaney vaala udhaaharan he jo rajya main chal rahi mithai kii dukaanon dwaara muhaiyaa karaae ja rahe hai or ye dukaane chaatr samudaay ko andhere main dhakelne ke liye jimmedaar hai
 Comments adaalat ne shiksha vibhaag ke ayukta or sachiv ko ek samiti gathit karne kaa nirdesh diya jo aisi digriyaan pesh karne vaale adhyapakon ko jaanch padtaal ke liye pesh hone ko kahegi or yah pataa lagaaegi ki kya unamem chaatro ko padhaane kii jaruri salaahiyat he
 The court also said, "those teachers who fail in such investigations, then their certificates should be confiscated after hearing their side
 prashasan ko chaatr samudaay or samaaj ke prati prakritik nyaay ke siddhant kaa anusaran karte hue unki sevaaon ko radd karnaa hoga
 The judge then asked the Director of School Education Department to send the case to the police station concerned for action in such cases
 justise mujffar hossain atar shuukravaar ko dakshini kashmir ke ek skool main mohammad imran khan ko rahabar-e-talim (shiksha guide) ke rup main niyukt kiye jane ko chunauti dene vaali yachika par sunwaayee kar rahe the
 The petitioner had alleged that Khan's certificates issued by the Board of Higher Secondary Education Delhi and Global Open University, Nagaland are not recognized
 dilli board dwaara jari kii gai marksheet darshaati he ki mohammad ne urdu, angraji or ganit main kramash: 74 fisadi, 73 fisadi or 66 fisadi ank hasil kiye the
 The court asked a senior lawyer to allow Mohammed to translate a simple line from English to Urdu and Urdu to English, but he failed to do so
 adhyaaapak ko iske baad gaay par urdu main niabandh likhane ko diya gaya, lekin vah ise bhi nahin likh paae
 Mohammed went out of the court room and asked for permission to write the essay, but even after getting approval, he could not write the essay
 ganit par acchhee pakad hone kaa daawa karne vaale mohammad ko is par chauthi kaksha kaa ganit kaa ek sawaal hal karne ko diya gaya
 Appearing distressed after his failure, Judge Atar said, 'in such a situation, what can be the future of the state can be estimated
 skool jane vaale bachche
 
 
 Even after passing, you will remain foolish
 ' The court said in its remarks, "the administration in the state of Jammu and Kashmir has the responsibility to ensure that the field of education and academics is not polluted, but looking at the facts revealed in this case, it is evident that the administration has taken the discretionary body and They have worked blindly, because they have made a criminal mistake by ignoring the terrible mistakes made in acquiring academic degrees
 ' nyaayadhish atar ne ayogy ummidavaaron ko praaanpatr muhaiyaa karaane vaale adhyayan kendron ko 'mithai kii dukaan' qaraar diya
 He said, "the current writ petition is a shocking example of the sale of academic degrees which are being provided by the sweets shops operating in the state and these shops are responsible for pushing the student community into darkness
" 'tippaniyan The court directed the Commissioner and Secretary of the Department of Education to set up a committee that would ask teachers presenting such degrees to appear for investigation and find out if they had the necessary mentorship to teach students
 adaalat ne yah bhi kaha, 'aise teacher jo is tarah kii jaanch main fail ho jate hai to unka paksh sunne ke baad unke praaanpatron ko jabt kiya jaae
 The administration will have to cancel their services, following the principle of natural justice towards the student community and society
